	             [],
	             [{temp,2},{temp,3},{temp,4}],
	             0,

	              {eval,{temp,3},{icon,222}},

	              {eval,{temp,4},{icon,1}},
	              {jump,{label,102}},

	          {12,"  addi = lb;"},
	          {13,"}"},
	          {14,[]},

	       {proc,{label,"mov"},

### ducc -t suite/quiet/semantic/s02.c gives:

	{{source,[{1,"int a;"},
	          {2,"int foo(int x) {"},
	          {3,"  ; }"},
	          {4,[]},
	          {5,"int main(void) {"},
	          {6,"  a = foo(a);\t"},
	          {7,"}"}]},
	 {rtl,[{data,{label,100},4},
	       {proc,{label,"foo"},[{temp,2}],[],0,[],{labdef,{label,101}}},
	       {proc,{label,"main"},
	             [],
	             [{temp,3},{temp,4},{temp,5},{temp,6}],
	             0,
	             [{'SOURCE',6,"  a = foo(a);\t"},
	              {eval,{temp,3},{labref,{label,100}}},
	              {load,long,{temp,4},{temp,3}},
	              {call,{temp,5},{label,"foo"},[{temp,4}]},
	              {eval,{temp,6},{labref,{label,100}}},
	              {store,long,{temp,6},{temp,5}}],
	             {labdef,{label,102}}}]}}.



### ducc -t suite/quiet/semantic/s03.c gives:

	{{source,[{1,[]},
	          {2,"int a[10];"},
	          {3,[]},
	          {4,"int foo(int x[]) {"},
	          {5,"  return x[0];"},
	          {6,"}"},
	          {7,[]},
	          {8,"int main(void) {"},
	          {9,"  foo(a);\t"},
	          {10,"}"}]},
	 {rtl,[{data,{label,100},40},
	       {proc,{label,"foo"},
	             [{temp,2}],
	             [{temp,3},{temp,4},{temp,5},{temp,6},{temp,7}],
	             0,
	             [{'SOURCE',5,"  return x[0];"},
	              {eval,{temp,3},{icon,0}},
	              {eval,{temp,4},{icon,4}},
	              {eval,{temp,5},{binop,'*',{temp,3},{temp,4}}},
	              {eval,{temp,6},{binop,'+',{temp,2},{temp,5}}},
	              {load,long,{temp,7},{temp,6}},
	              {eval,{temp,0},{temp,7}},
	              {jump,{label,101}}],
	             {labdef,{label,101}}},
	       {proc,{label,"main"},
	             [],
	             [{temp,8},{temp,9}],
	             0,
	             [{'SOURCE',9,"  foo(a);\t"},
	              {eval,{temp,8},{labref,{label,100}}},
	              {call,{temp,9},{label,"foo"},[{temp,8}]}],
	             {labdef,{label,102}}}]}}.

### ducc -t suite/quiet/semantic/s06.c gives:

	{{source,[{1,"int main(void) {"},
	          {2,"  char x;"},
	          {3,"  int y;"},
	          {4,"  "},
	          {5,"  x = y;"},
	          {6,"  y = x;"},
	          {7,"}"}]},

	             [],
	             [{temp,2},{temp,3}],
	             0,
	             [{'SOURCE',5,"  x = y;"},
	              {eval,{temp,2},{temp,3}},
	              {'SOURCE',6,"  y = x;"},
	              {eval,{temp,3},{temp,2}}],
	             {labdef,{label,100}}}]}}.
